name:A‚Äçi‚Äçs‚Äçu‚Äçi‚Äçs‚Äçu‚Äçi‚Äçn‚Äçi‚Äça‚Äçn‚Äçd‚Äçe‚Äçl‚Äçi‚Äçs‚Äça‚Äçn‚Äçs‚Äçu‚Äçi
info:Superior 2-bed Room
info:Stayed in February 2023
info:Family
info:2 Reviews
rating:3.5
posted:Posted February 10, 2023
msg:It was the first time I traveled during the epidemic in three years. I chose Wyndham Grand, a relatively new local star hotel, at night in Tongren. How can I put it this way? It was not a particularly good experience. I feel that the hotel can improve a lot (from Review habits of former hotel staff), but it is still a good hotel in the local area.

Facilities: The hotel is relatively new, so the facilities and equipment are relatively new, and the intelligence is also well done, such as electric curtains and smart lighting. Regarding the facilities, I think the main problem is the bathroom. The bathroom is relatively small. If you close the door and go to the bathroom, you will feel aggrieved. But the toilet is a smart toilet, which is a plus. There is also the fact that the TV can be cast from the mobile phone, which is very cool, but the TV does not have to be wired, which means that it can only be cast from the mobile phone. Although there are fewer people watching TV now, this most basic facility should be done well.

Hygiene: There are no old problems in a new hotel, so the overall hygiene is okay, at least within the reach of the naked eye, and there are no stains or spots that have not been cleaned properly.

Environment: There is a shopping mall downstairs of the hotel. There are supermarkets and Ruixing in it, as well as places to eat and drink. But the hotel room is facing an unfinished building, really, it makes people feel bad. Behind the hotel is a residential area similar to demolition, with many supper stalls. Whether this is good or not varies from person to person.

Service: The service of the staff is good or bad. When I checked in at the beginning, the guy at the front desk told me to wait a while, and then asked me to go to the lady who checked in with the previous guest next to me. This behavior is nothing wrong Question, but when the front desk of the hotel really asks guests to check in at another counter, can they not be so blunt, and feel a little bit like being called around. The attitude of the lady who changed was much better, and the speed was very fast. After asking how much it would cost to upgrade the deluxe room, she told me that she could check the room situation and help with the upgrade for free if possible, but I hope to give a good review. There is nothing wrong with this, but after the upgrade, you can tell the customer that you are welcome to check in after the upgrade. It is more convenient to "take credit" from the guests, instead of being a good person by yourself, after all, it is more difficult for the guests to see from the room Find out whether this is the advanced or upgraded deluxe room that I booked. But there is a service problem. I didn‚Äôt tell the guests whether the room included breakfast after check-in, which made me feel that I booked a room with breakfast. I ran to the restaurant for breakfast the next day and paid more than 140 yuan. Of course, first of all, this is my own problem. I was distracted when I made the reservation, but if I can remind me when I check in, at least I won‚Äôt rush into the breakfast room the next day. The increased breakfast of more than 140 is really unpalatable, and it is not as good as the noodles for 10 yuan outside. Distressed very much. Finally, what made me a little angry was that the front desk charged me the wrong fee for breakfast, and the deposit for the pre-sale right was deducted less, so they called me to inform me, because I asked the front desk to add me on WeChat on the expressway. I will pay the money after the high speed. When I got off the expressway and added WeChat, no one paid any attention to me. After looking at Alipay, I have already deducted more money from my Ctrip mortgage. Seriously, can this work? I chose to use my credit as a mortgage not to pay the room fee first, and pay after check-in, but the hotel can adjust the deduction amount at will without prior notice, nor does it require my consent, and Ctrip didn't remind me? If this is the case, everyone should pay attention to using this credit mortgage to check in, and you may be deducted inexplicably. And in this way, why bother me to swipe the pre-sale right when I check in? You can debit my account anyway you want. And the so-called personal butler who added my WeChat, there is no communication at all. This is really not acceptable.

Final summary: Tongren is a relatively new hotel with good facilities. The price/performance ratio will be higher if you don't eat breakfast, including breakfast, especially the extra is not worthwhile. The surrounding environment is very general, but it is convenient. The service is relatively unsatisfactory. But you do see staff working hard to serve customers.
ps. Forgetting to take a photo is a failure
